			Track Group Court Report Data Elements Guide			
			Agency			Name of the Agency as entered into the Intellitrack system
			Officer			Name of the assigned Supervision Officer as entered into the Intellitrack system
			Monitored Individual			Name of the Monitored Person as entered into the Intellitrack system
			Event Name			Abbreviated name of the event as used within the Intellitrack system
			Event Time UTC			Timestamp of the location event in Universal Time Coordinated (UTC), which is the time used by Intellitrack s devices and servers. UTC is the international standards name for Greenwich Mean Time (GMT).
			Event Time Local			Timestamp of the location event represented in agencys timezone and daylight savings context (adjusted from UTC).
			Latitude			The latitude coordinate associated with the alarm event as stored by the Intellitrack system
			Longitude			The longitude coordinate associated with the alarm event as stored by the Intellitrack system
			Derived Location			The ReverseGeoCoded street address of the event as provided by our GeoCoding provider. In the event that a latitude and longitude did not resolve to an address at the time of the event, the latitude and longitude will be displayed instead of a street address.
			GPS Satellite Count			Number of satellites used in the GPS positional fix
			HDOP			horizontal dilution of precision which is a GPS related metric. It refers to the GPS modules confidence in the horizontal positioning of the GPS fix
			GPS Confidence			The outcome of Intellitrack s GPS filtering mechanisms for a given latitude/longitude coordinate pairs accuracy. This field is calculated within the spreadsheet based on the values contained in the GPS Valid and GPS Valid Satellites fields. Confidence level of the GPS derived location is displayed as High, Medium, or Invalid
			Direction of Travel			Direction of travel calculated from the Device Heading Degrees field
			Device Heading Degrees			Direction of travel reported in degrees where 0 degrees is North and 180 degrees is South
			Device Speed MPH			The speed of travel as reported by the GPS module, in units of miles per hour
